<script>
    /*
    * Facebook Triggers
    */
    var pltFacebookPixel = false;

    jQuery(document).on('onProductImpressions',function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendImpressions();
    });

    jQuery(document).on('onProductView',function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendProductView();
    });

    jQuery(document).on('onAddToCart',function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendAddToCart();
    });

    jQuery(document).on('onPurchaseSuccess',function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendPurchaseSuccess();
    });

    jQuery(document).on('beforeunload',function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendTags();
    });

    jQuery(document).on('onBeforeCheckout',function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendInitiateCheckout();
    });

    window.onload = function(){
        if (!pltFacebookPixel) pltFacebookPixel = new PltFacebookPixel();
        pltFacebookPixel.sendTags();
    };

</script>    <script>

    <script>

        (function($) {
            $('.currency-link').on('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                const locale = $(this).data('locale');
                const currency = $(this).data('currency');
                const link = $('head').find('link[hreflang="' + locale + '"]');
                const querystring = $(this).data('querystring');
                let redirect = $(link).attr("href") + "?currency=" + currency + "&qs=" + querystring;
                if (typeof $(link).attr("href")  === 'undefined') {
                    redirect = $(this).attr("href");
                }
                window.location.href = redirect;
            });
        })(jQuery);

    </script>
                      </li>

<script>

	jQuery(document).ready(function() {

		var locale = 'en_GB';
		var currencySymbol = '£';
		var exchangeRate = 1;
		var baseUrl = 'https://www.prettylittlething.com/';

		/* This should be read from the config via PHP rather
		 than being hardcoded in here, but the properties have
		 been kept the same to make this an easy addition for
		 later on.
		 */

		/* Like other currency_data portions, this needs to be refactored
		 to account for different countries, ie New Zealand and Canada
		 that do not have their own locale right now
		 */

		var currency_data = {

			'en_GB': {
				'price':'price_gbp',
				'special':'special_price_gbp',
				'final':'slider_price_gbp_max'
			},

			'en_AU': {
				'price':'price_aud',
				'special':'special_price_aud',
				'final':'slider_price_aud_max'
			},

			'en_US': {
				'price':'price_usd',
				'special':'special_price_usd',
				'final':'slider_price_usd_max'
			},

			'en_IE': {
				'price':'price_eur',
				'special':'special_price_eur',
				'final':'slider_price_eur_max'
			}

		};

		var fredhopper = new Fredhopper();

		fredhopper.initialise({
			currency_data:currency_data,
			locale:locale,
			currency_symbol:currencySymbol,
			exchange_rate: exchangeRate,
			base_url:baseUrl
		});

		 var searchSuggest = new SearchSuggest();


		 searchSuggest.initialise({
		 	dataSource:fredhopper,
		 	selector: {
		 		searchContainer:'.page-search-container',
		 		searchTerm:'#searchbox',
		 		searchSuggest:'#search-suggest',
		 		clearButton:'.top-search-bar .btn-clear'
		 	}
		 });

        try {
            if (plt.cookies.readNamedCookie('pltsytesearch') == 1) {
                var syteHtml = '<a href="javascript:void();" class="--syte-start-camera-upload search-by-image" aria-label="Search" data-camera-button-placement="search-bar"><span class="fa fa-camera-retro" aria-hidden="true"></span></a>\n';
                jQuery('#sytesearch').html(syteHtml);
            }
        } catch (e) {}

	});

</script>

            <div class="filter filter-container slider" facetId="price"
                 data-facetFhId="99f4b390-a2cf-4f60-9db7-d1e55dfbb1e1">

            <div class="">

                <h6 class="toggle-category-header">
                    <i class="fa fa-caret-down" data-icon="caret"></i>
                                        Price                                  </h6>

                                    <span class="clr-btn hidden">clear</span>
                

            </div>


          <div class="filter-wraper-sub">



              
                  <div>
                      <div class="price-facet">

    <div class="price-slider"></div>

    <div class="labels">
                <div class="label priceFrom">£<span class="value"></span></div>
        <div class="label priceTo">£<span class="value"></span></div>
            </div>

</div>


<script>

    var priceSlider;

    jQuery( function() {

        priceSlider = PriceSlider({
            minValue:1,
            maxValue:27,
            valueFrom:1,
            valueTo:27,
            exchangeRate:1,
            minId:"99f4b390-a2cf-4f60-9db7-d1e55dfbb1e1",
            maxId:"6bc5796a-4a91-4f25-9856-5c90976ed09a",
        });

        priceSlider.drawPriceLabels();

    });

</script>


<script>

    var PriceSlider = function(data) {

        var me = {};

        var minValue = data.minValue;
        var maxValue = data.maxValue;
        var valueFrom = data.valueFrom;
        var valueTo = data.valueTo;
        var exchangeRate = data.exchangeRate;
        var startingValueFrom = data.valueFrom;
        var startingValueTo = data.valueTo;


        if (exchangeRate!==1) {
            exchangeRate=exchangeRate;
        }

        var rounding = 5;
        if (valueFrom==minValue) {
            minValue = minValue > 1 ? Math.floor((minValue/rounding)*rounding) : minValue;
            valueFrom = minValue;
        } else {
            minValue = minValue > 1 ? Math.floor((minValue/rounding)*rounding) : minValue;
        }

        if (valueTo==maxValue) {
            maxValue = Math.floor((maxValue/rounding)*rounding);
            valueTo = maxValue;
        } else {
            maxValue = Math.ceil((maxValue/rounding)*rounding);
        }

        jQuery( ".price-facet .price-slider" ).slider({
            range: true,
            min: minValue,
            max: maxValue,
            values: [ valueFrom, valueTo ],
            isRTL: false,
            slide: function( event, ui ) {
                this.onSlide(ui.values[0],ui.values[1], startingValueFrom, startingValueTo);
            }.bind(me)
        });

        var t1;

        me.onSlide = function(v1, v2, from, to) {

            this.updatePrices(v1,v2);
            this.drawPriceLabels();
            if (this.timer) {
                clearTimeout(this.timer);
            }
            var that = this;
            this.timer = setTimeout(function() { that.track(v1, v2, from, to); }, 300);
            plt.categoryView.onFacetChange();
        };

        me.track = function(v1, v2, from, to) {
            if (v1 !== from) {
                this.pushEvent('priceSlide', v1, this.getMinId());
            }
            if (v2 !== to) {
                this.pushEvent('priceSlide', v2, this.getMaxId());
            }
        }

        me.pushEvent = function (event, value, id) {
            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event': event,
                'facetId': id,
                'facetValue': '' + value
            });
        }

        me.clearSelection = function() {

            valueFrom = minValue;
            valueTo = maxValue;

            jQuery(".price-facet .price-slider").slider('values',[valueFrom,valueTo]);

            this.drawPriceLabels();

        }.bind(me);

        me.hasSelection = function() {

            if ((valueFrom!=minValue) || (valueTo!=maxValue)) {
                return true;
            }

            return false;

        }.bind(me);

        me.updatePrices = function(p1,p2) {
            valueFrom = p1;
            valueTo = p2;
        }.bind(me);

        me.drawPriceLabels = function() {
            jQuery('.label.priceFrom .value').html(me.convertValueForDisplay(valueFrom,false));
            jQuery('.label.priceTo .value').html(me.convertValueForDisplay(valueTo,true));

        }.bind(me);

        me.convertValueForDisplay = function(v,r) {

            var displayValue = v * exchangeRate;

            if (r) {
                displayValue = Math.ceil(displayValue);
            } else {
                displayValue = (displayValue > 1 || displayValue == 0.01) ? Math.floor(displayValue) : (Math.floor(displayValue * 10) * 10 / 100).toFixed(2);
            }

            return displayValue;

        };

        me.getValueFrom = function() {
            return valueFrom;
        }.bind(me);

        me.getValueTo = function() {
            return valueTo;
        }.bind(me);

        me.getMinValue = function() {
            return minValue;
        }.bind(me);

        me.getMaxValue = function() {
            return maxValue;
        }.bind(me);

        me.getMinId = function() {
            return data.minId;
        }.bind(me);

        me.getMaxId = function() {
            return data.maxId;
        }.bind(me);


        return me;
    }

</script>
                  </div>

                        </div>


        </div>

        
      </dl>

    </div>

  </div>
</div>


        </div>
        <main class="col-sm-9 col-md-10 page-main">
            <div class="cookie-preference__overlay">

</div>

    jQuery(document).ready(function() {
        if (Mage.Cookies.get('pltbvcontent') != 1) {
            jQuery('.bv-content').hide();
        }
        jQuery(document).on('loadMoreSuccess', function() {
            if (Mage.Cookies.get('pltbvcontent') != 1) {
                jQuery('.bv-content').hide();
            }
        })
    });

<script id='trackingloader' type='txt/template'>

    <div id='trackingloader'>
        <img src="https://cdn-skin.prettylittlething.com/frontend/prettylittlething/plt-theme/images/opc-ajax-loader.gif?ts=1681834602"
             alt="Please wait..."
             title="Please wait..."
             class="v-middle"/> Please wait...</img>
    </div>

</script>

<script>
    jQuery(function () {

        jQuery('.trackmyorder').on('click', function () {

            var parent = jQuery(this).parent();

            var html = jQuery('#trackingloader').html();

            // Set spinner
            jQuery('#trackingloader').before('#trackmyorder').show();

            var orderNo = parent.find('.orderRef').val();
            var formKey = parent.find('.tracking_form_key').val();

            jQuery.ajax({
                method: 'POST',
                url: "/customer/tracking/gettrackingurl",
                data: {'orderNo': orderNo, 'form_key': formKey},
                dataType: 'json'
            }).complete(function (data) {

                data = data.responseJSON;

                if (data.status == 0) {

                    var url = data.redirectUrl;
                    window.location = url;

                } else {

                    // remove spinner
                    parent.find('#trackingloader').hide();

                    // show error message
                    var msg = data.msg;

                    parent.find('.tracking-error').remove(0);
                    if (parent.hasClass('delivery-tracking')) {
                        parent.find('.trackmyorder').after('<div class="tracking-error">' + msg + '</div>');
                    } else {
                        parent.find('.trackmyorder').before('<div class="tracking-error">' + msg + '</div>');
                    }

                    parent.find('.tracking-error').delay(5000).hide(0);

                }

            });
        });
    });
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var formsToProtectOnPage = [];
        var currentForm;
        var currentValidationForm;
        var checkedForms = [];
        var hasFormsChanged = false;

        var onSubmit = function (token) {
            if (currentValidationForm && currentValidationForm.validator
                && currentValidationForm.validator.validate()
            ) {
                currentForm.querySelector('[name="amasty_invisible_token"]').setAttribute('value', token);
                if (typeof(recaptchaObject) !== 'undefined') {
                    recaptchaObject.submit();
                } else {
                    currentForm.submit();
                }
            } else {
                grecaptcha.reset();
            }
        };

        function checkForms() {
            formsToProtect = ["form[action*=\"contact-us\/index\/post\"]","form[action*=\"exponea\"]"];
            formsToProtect.forEach(function (item) {
                var continueWorking = true;
                formsSearchedBySelector = $$(item);
                checkedForms.forEach(function(element) {
                    if (element[0] == formsSearchedBySelector[0]) {
                        continueWorking = false;
                        return;
                    }
                })
                if (formsSearchedBySelector.length != 0 && continueWorking) {
                    checkedForms.push(formsSearchedBySelector);
                    formsSearchedBySelector.forEach(function (formToProtect) {
                        formsToProtectOnPage.push(formToProtect);
                        hasFormsChanged = true;
                    });
                }
            });
            if (hasFormsChanged) {
                for (var index in formsToProtectOnPage) {
                    if (formsToProtectOnPage.hasOwnProperty(index)) {
                        var formToProtectOnPage = formsToProtectOnPage[index];
                        if ('form' !== formToProtectOnPage.tagName.toLowerCase()) {
                            formToProtectOnPage = formToProtectOnPage.getElementsByTagName('form');
                            if (0 < formToProtectOnPage.length) {
                                formToProtectOnPage = formToProtectOnPage[0];
                            } else {
                                continue;
                            }
                        }

                        if (formToProtectOnPage.getElementsByClassName("amasty_recaptcha").length == 0) {
                            var recaptchaBlock = document.createElement('div');
                            recaptchaBlock.className = 'amasty_recaptcha';
                            formToProtectOnPage.appendChild(recaptchaBlock);

                            var tokenInput = document.createElement('input');
                            tokenInput.type = 'hidden';
                            tokenInput.name = 'amasty_invisible_token';
                            tokenInput.value = '';
                            formToProtectOnPage.appendChild(tokenInput);
                        }

                        formToProtectOnPage.onsubmit = function submitProtectedForm(event) {
                            currentForm = event.target;
                            currentValidationForm = new VarienForm(currentForm.id, false);
                            recaptchaBlock = currentForm.querySelector(".amasty_recaptcha");
                            if ('' == recaptchaBlock.innerHTML) {
                                recaptcha = grecaptcha.render(recaptchaBlock, {
                                    'sitekey': '6LfhNM4aAAAAADRAbEOZSLE52t_Vk5B3-won7rKb',
                                    'callback': onSubmit,
                                    'size': 'invisible',
                                    'theme': 'light',
                                    'badge': 'bottomright'
                                });
                            }
                            grecaptcha.reset(recaptcha);
                            grecaptcha.execute(recaptcha);
                            return false;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        jQuery(document).ready(function() {
            var formsCount = 0;
            setInterval(function () {
                var formLength = $$('form').length;
                if (formsCount != formLength) {
                    formsCount = formLength;
                    checkForms();
                }
            }, 1000);
        });
    </script>
            <script src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js" async defer></script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
    dataLayer.push({
        'dwin-id':  '5577'
    });

    function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
        var result = null,
            tmp = [];
        location.search
            .substr(1)
            .split("&")
            .forEach(function (item) {
                tmp = item.split("=");
                if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
            });
        return result;
    }

    var utm_source = findGetParameter('utm_source');
    var utm_medium = findGetParameter('utm_medium');
    if (utm_source || utm_medium) {
        var cookieValue = "source=" + utm_source + "&" +"medium=" + utm_medium;
        var d = new Date();
        d.setTime(d.getTime() + 30*24*60*60*1000);
        var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
        document.cookie = "affiliateOrigin=" + cookieValue + "; " + expires + "; path=/" +";domain=.prettylittlething.com";
    }

</script><script type="text/javascript">
    if (!Mage.Cookies.get('nugg')) {
        new Ajax.Request('https://www.prettylittlething.com/nugg/', {
                onSuccess: function (transport) {
                    Mage.Cookies.set('nugg', 1);
                    if(document.getElementById('form_key')){
                        document.getElementById('form_key').value = transport._getResponseJSON();
                    }
                    if (document.getElementById('product_addtocart_form')) {
                        var action = document.getElementById('product_addtocart_form').action;
                        action = action.substring(0, action.length - 1);
                        document.getElementById('product_addtocart_form').action = action.replace(/[^\/]+$/, transport._getResponseJSON()) + '/';
                    }

                    // order tracking
                    var trackingFormKeys = document.getElementsByClassName('tracking_form_key');
                    if (trackingFormKeys.length) {
                        trackingFormKeys[0].value = transport._getResponseJSON();
                    }

                }
            }
        );
    }
</script>
